national_JJ or_CC local_JJ economic_JJ conditions_NNS that_WDT correlate_VBP with_IN defaults_NNS on_IN the_DT assets_NNS in_IN the_DT portfolio_NN ._.

a_DT Fair_NN value_NN hedges_NNS The_DT Group_NNP designates_VBZ a_DT number_NN of_IN derivatives_NNS as_IN fair_JJ values_NNS hedges_NNS ._.
